<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
/* This code is necessary so that the default text (marketing message) in the search field doesn't actually get
searched on if the user hits the search button without first entering text of their own.  This
ensures that the default search is made instead.  We do this by clearing out the default value of the search field before
firing off the search.
 */
 
var searchFieldFocused = false;
var searchboxvalue = "" + escape("What are you looking for? Find it here:");
function clearSearchField(id) {
if( escape(id.value) == searchboxvalue ) {
id.value = "";
searchFieldFocused = true;
}
}


function submitSearchForm(sid,nid,url,pageCodes,pages,enablePopResults,domain,popUpTitle,keepFocusInParent) {
//if the search field has not been clicked in, clear it
//of the default text before firing off the search
if( !searchFieldFocused && (escape(document.getElementById('searchTop-s2').value) == searchboxvalue) ) {
document.getElementById('searchTop-s2').value = "";
}
return submitStaticSearchLinkNew(sid,nid,url,pageCodes,pages,enablePopResults,domain,popUpTitle,keepFocusInParent);
}

//]]>
</script>

<input name="search" type="text" class="hv2-search-input hv2-dark-searchtext" id="searchTop-s2" value="dodge ram 2500 diesel transmission" onclick="clearSearchField(this);" />
<button id="search-button" title="Find it" type="submit"></button>
